WHEREAS, in accordance with the Constitution of the Azerbaijan Republic and the<br /><br />
Constitutional Act of State Independence of the Azerbaijan Republic, dated 18 October 1991, and<br /><br />
the Law on Ownership in the Azerbaijan Republic, dated 9 November 1991, ownership of all<br /><br />
mineral resources existing in its natural state is vested in the Azerbaijan Republic, and based upon<br /><br />
the referenced authorizations the authority to control and manage precious metals and minerals<br /><br />
including gold, silver, precious and semi-precious stones has been vested in AZERGYZIL; and<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />
Contractor shall within six (6) months following the Effective Date study all<br /><br />
information and data in the possession of AZERGYZIL, prepare and submit to AZERGYZIL a<br /><br />
detailed Program (the Exploration Work Program) to carry out exploration and appraisal of the<br /><br />
mineral resources in the Contract Area for each individual Mining Property. Along with the<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL resolution the Program shall be affirmed by the corresponding executive authorities.<br /><br />
If the Program isn’t affirmed within the period of one month and the Contractor does not agree<br /><br />
with the corresponding executive authorities, the said Program shall be examined by an<br /><br />
experienced Auditor company, invited by the AZERGYZIL and the Contractor. The Auditor's<br /><br />
reference on the Program shall be obligatory. The audit costs shall be included in the operational<br /><br />
expense and it is Cost Recoverable. However, in the event Contractor does not submit to<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL the Program to carry out exploration and appraisal of the mineral resources for any<br /><br />
of the Mining Properties in the Contract Area by the end of the said six (6) month period,<br /><br />
Contractor shall lose all rights pertaining to such Mining Property under this Agreement and costs<br /><br />
incurred by Contractor with respect to such Mining Property shall not be Cost Recoverable.<br /><br />

5.3<br /><br />
Contractor's failure to perform all or a portion of its obligations as set out in Article<br /><br />
5.2 during the Exploration Period with respect to any individual Mining Property other than as a<br /><br />
result of Force Majeure shall constitute a Material Breach by Contractor of its obligations under<br /><br />
this Agreement with respect to such particular individual Mining Property. In this case<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL has every right on its own consideration to terminate the Agreement with respect to<br /><br />
such individual Mining Property and all the costs incurred by Contractor shall not be Cost<br /><br />
Recoverable. The termination of the Contract on the part of AZERGYZIL in accordance with the<br /><br />
Article 5.3 is the only means of legal protection of AZERGYZIL against the Contractor for the<br /><br />
Material Breach. Such termination shall be without prejudice to any claims either AZERGYZIL or<br /><br />
Contractor may have which arose prior to such termination.<br /><br />

5.6<br /><br />
Because of occupation by the Armenian armed forces of the territories of Soutely<br /><br />
Mining Property, Kyzlbulag Mining Property and Vejnaly Mining Property the Preliminary<br /><br />
Period, Exploration Period and Additional Exploration Period referred to in this Article 5 shall be<br /><br />
realized when the mentioned territories are liberated; then the preparation period for the programs<br /><br />
for the Preliminary Period, Exploration Period and Additional Exploration Period shall be<br /><br />
automatically extended for six (6) months, such extension to begin on the date that AZERGYZIL<br /><br />
provides notice to Contractor that the Organization on Security and Cooperation in Europe<br /><br />
(OSCE) or a comparable international organization acknowledges a liberation of the mentioned<br /><br />
territories and cessation from all hostilities.<br /><br />

such Discovery and its Commerciality to extend the boundaries of such Mining Properties,<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL shall make every effort to grant the additional areas to Contractor and if granted<br /><br />
such additional areas shall become the subject of this Agreement.<br /><br />

áåø (15) ýöí êå÷ í ä ê ýþðöøöðë ð. Ïîäðàä÷û ìöçàêèð í òèæ ñèíä ðàçûëàøäûðûëìûø áöòöí<br /><br />

àëòìûø (60) ýöí ðçèíä ÀÇßÐÃÛÇÛË ù ð ùàíñû áèð éàòàã ö÷öí Èøë íì â ùàñèëàò<br /><br />

ñîíðàêû ãûðõ (40) ýöí ðçèíä àðáèòðàú àðàøäûðìàñûíà áàøëàéà áèë ð. ßý ð àðáèòðë ðèí<br /><br />
ã ðàðûíäà ÀÇßÐÃÛÇÛË-ûí Èøë íì â ùàñèëàò ïðîãðàìûíû ò ñäèã åòì êä í ñàññûç îëàðàã<br /><br />

áèë ð. Ëàêèí ý ð àðáèòð ã ðàðû ÷ûõàðûëàíäàí ñîíðà àëòû (6) àé ðçèíä Ïîäðàò÷û Èøë íì â<br /><br />
ùàñèëàò ïðîãðàìûíà óéüóí îëàðàã ëàùèää ýþòöðöëìöø ù ð ùàíñû áèð éàòàüûí Ì 'ä í-ôèëèç<br /><br />
ì ëèééàòëàðûíà áàøëàìûðñà, éóõàðûäà ýþñò ðèë í äþâðä í ñîíðà àëòìûø (60) ýöí ðçèíä<br /><br />
ÀÇßÐÃÛÇÛË-ûí èõòèéàðû âàð êè, Ïîäðàò÷ûéà éàçûëû áèëäèðèø ýþíä ðèá áó Ñàçèøèí ù ìèí<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(c)<br /><br />
The Development and Production Program shall be a long range plan for the<br /><br />
efficient and prompt development and production of mineral resources for each individual Mining<br /><br />
Property to produce Commercial Products in accordance with International Mining Industry<br /><br />
Standards and shall include but not be limited to the following:<br /><br />
an outline or map of the surface extent of the Ore Deposit located on the applicable<br /><br />
topographical maps together with the related geological and technical data;<br /><br />
an estimate of the geologic reserves in place (tonnage and grade), the estimated mineable<br /><br />
reserves contained therein, an estimate of the recoverable reserves and the corresponding estimated<br /><br />
annual production, together with a study of the proposed methods of recovery and possible<br /><br />
commercialization of the Commercial Products contained in the Ore Deposit;<br /><br />
a description of the requisite plant, equipment, supplies and work necessary for the mining,<br /><br />
milling, smelting, refining and minting of the Commercial Products therefrom;<br /><br />
the estimated schedule for implementation and the projected date of production start-up;<br /><br />
the estimates of capital investment required, operating capital needed and exploitation costs<br /><br />
together with economic projections demonstrating the commercial viability of the Ore Deposit;<br /><br />
and<br /><br />
a description of the work necessary to rehabilitate and abandon the lands and assets<br /><br />
impacted by Mining Operations (in accordance with International Mining Industry Standards),<br /><br />
including a detailed estimate of the funds necessary to finance such work.<br /><br />
(d)<br /><br />
Within thirty (30) days of receipt of the Development and Production Program<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL may request Contractor to provide such further information as is readily available<br /><br />
and as AZERGYZIL may reasonably need to evaluate the Development and Production Program.<br /><br />
(e)<br /><br />
Unless AZERGYZIL requests in writing to Contractor any changes to the<br /><br />
Development and Production Program within ninety (90) days of formal receipt thereof, the<br /><br />
Development and Production Program shall be deemed acceptable to AZERGYZIL.<br /><br />
In the event that AZERGYZIL requests any changes to the said Program then the<br /><br />
Parties shall meet within fifteen (15) days of receipt by Contractor of AZERGYZIL's written<br /><br />
notification of requested changes and shall discuss such request. Any agreed revision to the said<br /><br />
Program shall be incorporated into the Program by Contractor. In the event that the Development<br /><br />
and Production Program for each individual Mining Property has not been approved by<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL within sixty (60) days of the commencement of such discussion, Contractor may<br /><br />
within a further forty (40) days commence arbitration under the Arbitration Procedure on the<br /><br />
question as to whether or not AZERGYZYL's approval of the development and production<br /><br />
program has been unreasonably withheld. If the decision of Contractor’s arbitrators is that<br /><br />
approval was withheld by AZERGYZIL unreasonably Contractor shall be entitled to commence<br /><br />
Mining Operations in accordance with the said Development and Production Program in all<br /><br />

ðàçûëàøäûðìàã;<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />

êîìèòÿíèí ñÿäðè èëÿ ðàçûëàøäûðäûãäàí ñîíðà Ðÿùáÿð êîìèòÿíèí áöòöí öçâëÿðè àðàñûíäà éàéìàã.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(a)<br /><br />
The Steering Committee shall be comprised of an equal number of members from<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL and Contractor: three (3) representatives appointed by AZERGYZIL and three (3)<br /><br />
representatives appointed by Contractor, provided that the Parties shall each advise the other of the<br /><br />
names, place of work and position of its representatives. In the event of disease or absence or any<br /><br />
other reason whatsoever of any representative appointed by the Parties to participate at the<br /><br />
Steering Committee meetings and for the purpose of a quorum (consisting of three (3)<br /><br />
representatives from each Party present either in person or by telephone conference call) each<br /><br />
Party shall be entitled to appoint an alternate for each of its representatives to the Steering<br /><br />
Committee.<br /><br />
Such representatives and their alternates may be replaced by the Party upon written notice<br /><br />
to the other.<br /><br />
(b)<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL and Contractor shall each have one (1) vote to cast at the Steering<br /><br />
Committee meetings and decisions of the Steering Committee shall require the affirmative vote of<br /><br />
representatives as authorized to cast vote of both Parties. Each of the Parties shall give written<br /><br />
notice to the other specifying the identity of the individual representative, who shall be authorized<br /><br />
to cast such vote on its behalf.<br /><br />
(c)<br /><br />
The chairman of the Steering Committee shall be appointed by AZERGYZIL from one of<br /><br />
its appointed representatives to the Steering Committee and shall be entitled together with the<br /><br />
secretary to sign any minutes as agreed between the Parties and resolutions of the Steering<br /><br />
Committee.<br /><br />
(d)<br /><br />
The secretary to the Steering Committee shall be appointed by Contractor from one of its<br /><br />
appointed representatives to the Steering Committee and shall be responsible for:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
the production of an agenda of each Steering Committee meeting, such agenda to<br /><br />
be agreed between the Parties;<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
the production of minutes, which minutes shall be approved by the chairman of the<br /><br />
Steering Committee and circulation of minutes of the Steering Committee meeting among all<br /><br />
representatives.<br /><br />
(e)<br /><br />
Each Party shall be entitled to send advisers and experts to meetings of the Steering<br /><br />
Committee. Unless the Steering Committee agrees, the cost of such advisors and experts in<br /><br />
attending the meetings shall not be Cost Recoverable.<br /><br />

The Steering Committee will meet at least two (2) times in a Calendar Year. Meetings shall<br /><br />

(g)<br /><br />
Each Party shall have the right to call additional meetings of the Steering Committee upon<br /><br />
fifteen (15) days prior written notice to each other.<br /><br />
6.3<br /><br />
Annual Work Programs and Budgets<br /><br />
Not more than thirty (30) days following the formation of the Steering Committee and<br /><br />
thereafter at least three (3) months before the beginning of each Calendar Year during the<br /><br />
Development and Production Period, Contractor shall prepare and submit to the Steering<br /><br />
Committee for review and approval an Annual Work Program together with the related Budget in<br /><br />
respect of the Mining Operations Contractor proposes to be carried out in such a calendar year.<br /><br />
The Steering Committee shall meet within thirty (30) days of receipt of the Annual Work Program<br /><br />
and Budget to consider same and any revisions thereto and to approve the Annual Work Program<br /><br />
and the Budget in its final form. Thus Contractor shall fulfill the Annual Work Program and<br /><br />
related Budget and shall not conduct any operations which deviate from the Annual Work Program<br /><br />

and related Budget, however, as the work proceeds new data or information acquired may justify<br /><br />
changes or modifications to the details of the Annual Work Program and related Budget: thus<br /><br />
Contractor may propose amendments or modifications to the Annual Work Program and related<br /><br />
Budget and shall submit such amendments or modifications to the Steering Committee for review<br /><br />
to amend or modify the Annual Work Program and related Budget subject to the Steering<br /><br />
Committee approval.<br /><br />
If necessary to carry out an Annual Work Program, Contractor is authorized to make<br /><br />
expenditures during the relevant Calendar Year that are in excess of the Budget adopted therefore<br /><br />
so long as the aggregate of such excess expenditures does not exceed ten (10) percent of the<br /><br />
Budget unless such expenditures exceeding ten (10) percent are approved by the Steering<br /><br />
Committee.<br /><br />
In accordance with the other provisions of this Agreement, after approval of an Annual<br /><br />
Work Program and Budget, Contractor shall conduct the Mining Operations in accordance<br /><br />
therewith.<br /><br />
6.4. In the event the Annual Work Program and Budget has not been approved by the Steering<br /><br />
Committee by the first days of the Calendar Year to which it relates Contractor shall be entitled,<br /><br />
but not obligated to carry out Mining Operations in accordance with some or all of its proposed<br /><br />
Annual Work Program and Budget until such time as the Annual Work Program and Budget is<br /><br />
agreed by the Steering Committee or any dispute relating to the Annual Work Program and Budget<br /><br />
has been resolved by reference to arbitration in accordance with the Arbitration Procedures. As<br /><br />
soon as agreement on an Annual Work Program and Budget is reached by the Steering Committee<br /><br />
or the decision of the arbiters is rendered, Contractor shall amend the then current and/or next<br /><br />
following Annual Work Program and Budget, as appropriate, to conform with such agreement or<br /><br />
decision; provided that Contractor shall not be obligated to undo work already performed , may<br /><br />
complete any work in progress to the extent Contractor deems necessary and that all costs incurred<br /><br />
by Contractor in performing Mining Operations under its proposed Annual Work Program and<br /><br />
Budget shall be deemed to be Mining Costs subject to Cost Recovery under this Agreement.<br /><br />
The foregoing notwithstanding, if the arbitration award is issued in favor of either Party,<br /><br />
Contractor shall be entitled to Cost Recovery of the following items:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
ongoing commitments of Contractor, including contracts entered into prior to the<br /><br />
initiation of any such arbitration; and<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
work, Contractor considers necessary for the protection of the mine workings,<br /><br />
equipment, communication systems and facilities as used for and in relation to Mining Operations;<br /><br />
and<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
work Contractor considers necessary for the protection of the environment, health<br /><br />
and safety.<br /><br />
6.5 Emergency Measures<br /><br />
Notwithstanding any provision of this Agreement to the contrary, in the case of an<br /><br />
emergency or anticipated emergency, Contractor shall take all measures reasonably considered<br /><br />
necessary by Contractor for the protection of life, health, the environment and property.<br /><br />
The costs of taking such measures shall be included automatically as an approved addition<br /><br />
to the then current Budget and shall be deemed to be Mining Costs subject to Cost Recovery under<br /><br />
this Agreement, unless such accident or other emergency was the result of Contractor's Willful<br /><br />
Misconduct.<br /><br />

provided such costs are supported by appropriate documentary evidence. Contractor shall<br /><br />
reimburse AZERGYZIL for such expense, without creating any profit or loss for the latter.<br /><br />

available to Contractor all other land necessary to carry out Mining Operations under control of the<br /><br />
Third Parties or the Governmental Authorities including, but not limited to, the road construction,<br /><br />
aerial and/or cable power transmission, communication systems, buildings, facilities and the like.<br /><br />

accordance with legislation of the Azerbaijan Republic.<br /><br />

AZERGYZIL'S Assistance<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor Facilities<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor shall be responsible for the design, repair, refurbishment, upgrading of all<br /><br />
facilities controlled and operated by Contractor, including rent fees in connection with Mining<br /><br />
Operations (Contractor Facilities). Fees from Third Parties access to Contractor Facilities shall be<br /><br />
credited to the Mining Operations Account.<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL shall have the right to use excess capacity in Contractor Facilities provided<br /><br />
such use does not interfere with or adversely affect Mining Operations. Third Parties may use such<br /><br />
excess capacity on terms agreed with Contractor. Prior to Zero Balance the priority of such use of<br /><br />
Contractor Facilities shall be first Contractor, second Third Parties, and finally AZERGYZIL,<br /><br />
provided that AZERGYZIL and Third Parties may pay a mutually agreed fee for such use of<br /><br />
Contractors Facilities to be credited to the Mining Operations Account. Maintenance of Contractor<br /><br />
Facilities, for the time being not used by Contractor and being utilized exclusively by<br /><br />
AZERGYZIL, shall be on terms to be mutually agreed. Notwithstanding anything to the contrary<br /><br />
in this Agreement, Contractor shall have the right to dispose of equipment and facilities which for<br /><br />
the purpose of Mining Operations are either obsolete or are nearing the end of their useful<br /><br />
economic life, except in the case of fixed assets to which the provisions of Article 10.2(d) shall<br /><br />
apply by giving a prior written notice to AZERGYZIL of its intent. Unless AZERGYZIL elects,<br /><br />
within thirty (30) days to assume responsibility for and take delivery thereof, Contractor shall be<br /><br />
free to dispose of any such equipment and facilities at the best price obtainable. Funds from such<br /><br />
sales will be credited to the Mining Operations Account. Notwithstanding any provision herein to<br /><br />
the contrary, AZERGYZIL and Contractor shall have equal priority to capacity in Contractor<br /><br />
Facilities to store and to transport its share of Commercial Products.<br /><br />

OWNERSHIP, USE AND ABANDONMENT OF ASSETS<br /><br />
10.1<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Ownership and Use<br /><br />
Title to the following categories of fixed and moveable assets for use in Mining Operations<br /><br />
shall pass to AZERGYZIL in accordance with the following:<br /><br />
(a)<br /><br />
When legally permissible to purchase land, any land purchased by Contractor in the<br /><br />
Azerbaijan Republic for Mining Operations shall become the property of AZERGYZIL, as soon as<br /><br />
it is purchased.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(b)<br /><br />
Ìÿ'äÿí-ôèëèç ÿìÿëèééàòëàðûíäà Ïîäðàò÷ûíûí èñòèôàäÿ åòäèéè áöòöí ßñàñ ôîíäëàð âÿ<br /><br />
äàøûíàð ÿìëàê - áóíëàðûí äÿéÿðè Ìÿ'äÿí-ôèëèç ÿìÿëèééàòëàðû ö÷öí Ìÿñðÿôëÿðÿ àèä åäèëèð öçÿðèíäÿ ìöëêèééÿò ùöãóãó ÀÇßÐÃÛÇÛË-à àøàüûäà ýþñòÿðèëÿí òàðèõëÿð è÷ÿðèñèíäÿ ÿí åðêÿí<br /><br />
òàðèõäÿ êå÷èð:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
Ñûôûð áàëàíñûíà íàèë îëóíàíäàí ñîíðà ýÿëÿí Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëûíûí ñîíóíäà âÿ éà<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(b)<br /><br />
Title to fixed and moveable assets employed by Contractor in the performance of Mining<br /><br />

<br /><br />
CONTRACTORS RECOVERY OF MINING COSTS<br /><br />
AND PRODUCTION SHARING<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.1 Ïîäðàò÷ûíûí ùÿð áèð ÿëàùèääÿ Ìÿ'äÿí-ôèëèç éàòàüû öçðÿ Ìÿ'äÿí-ôèëèç ÿìÿëèééàòëàðûíà<br /><br />
÷ÿêäèéè Ìÿñðÿôëÿðèí ÿâÿçè Ëàéèùÿëÿøäèðèëÿí ìàëèééÿ äþâðèééÿñè ïðèíñèïè öçðÿ ùÿìèí ßëàùèääÿ<br /><br />

ñîíðàêû áÿíäëÿðèíèí ùàìûñûíà øàìèë åäèëèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
11.1 Contractor’s recovery of Mining Costs for each individual Mining Property shall be<br /><br />
achieved from Commercial Products of each individual Mining Property in a manner of Project<br /><br />
Financial Cycle, provided that such provision shall be applied to any clause of this Article 11.<br /><br />

11.4 Calculation of Cost Recovery and implementation of Cost Recovery shall be on a Calendar<br /><br />
Quarter basis.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(à)<br /><br />
Ùÿð Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëû ãóðòàðäûãäà Ìàëèééÿëÿøäèðìÿ ìÿñðÿôëÿðè, î æöìëÿäÿí ÿâÿçè<br /><br />
þäÿíèëìÿìèø ßñàñëû ìÿñðÿôëÿð âÿ ÿââÿëêè Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëûíäàí êå÷èðèëìèø, ëàêèí àäû ÷ÿêèëÿí<br /><br />
æàðè Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëûíäà ÿâÿçè þäÿíèëìÿìèø ßìÿëèééàò ìÿñðÿôëÿðè ÿâÿçè þäÿíèëìÿìèø ßñàñëû<br /><br />
ìÿñðÿôëÿðÿ âÿ/éàõóä ßìÿëèééàò ìÿñðÿôëÿðèíÿ ÿëàâÿ åäèëèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(a)<br /><br />
At the end of each Calendar Quarter, Finance Costs shall be applied to any unrecovered<br /><br />
Capital Costs and/or Operating Costs, including any unrecovered Capital Costs and Operating<br /><br />
Costs carried forward from any previous Calendar Quarter, which have not been recovered in such<br /><br />
current Calendar Quarter;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(b)<br /><br />
Ùÿð Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëû öçðÿ ÿâÿçè þäÿíèëìÿìèø ßñàñëû ìÿñðÿôëÿðèí ìàëèééÿëÿøäèðèëìÿñèíÿ<br /><br />

ßñàñëû ìÿñðÿôëÿðèí ñàëäîñó èëÿ æÿìëÿíèð âÿ ñîíðàëàð ßñàñëû ìÿñðÿôëÿð êèìè þäÿíèëèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(b)<br /><br />

the end of each Calendar Quarter, be aggregated with the unrecovered balance of Capital Costs at<br /><br />
that date and thereafter be recovered as Capital Costs;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(æ)<br /><br />
Ùÿð Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëû öçðÿ ÿâÿçè þäÿíèëìÿìèø ßìÿëèééàò ìÿñðÿôëÿðèíèí<br /><br />
ìàëèééÿëÿøäèðèëìÿñèíÿ ÷ÿêèëÿí õÿðæëÿð ùÿð Òÿãâèì êâàðòàëû ãóðòàðäûãäàí ñîíðà ùÿìèí ýöíÿäÿê<br /><br />
ÿâÿçè þäÿíèëìÿìèø ßìÿëèééàò ìÿñðÿôëÿðèíèí ñàëäîñó èëÿ æÿìëÿíèð âÿ ñîíðàëàð ßìÿëèééàò<br /><br />
ìÿñðÿôëÿðè êèìè þäÿíèëèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(c)<br /><br />
Finance Costs in respect of unrecovered Operating Costs for each Calendar Quarter shall,<br /><br />
at the end of each Calendar Quarter, be aggregated with the unrecovered balance of Operating<br /><br />
Costs at that date and thereafter be recovered as Operating Costs;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(d)<br /><br />
Ïîäðàò÷ûíûí Ìÿ'äÿí-ôèëèç ÿìÿëèééàòàðûíà ÷ÿêäèéè âÿ ÿâÿçè þäÿíèëìÿëè îëàí, ëàêèí ÿââÿëêè<br /><br />

With respect to metals, AZERGYZIL and Contractor shall weigh and sample on a monthly<br /><br />
basis all dore bars and containers of carbon materials or any other materials which may contain<br /><br />
precipitated metallic minerals produced from mining and milling operations prior to transporting<br /><br />
such dore bars or containers to the Processing Point. Such measurements shall be verified by an<br /><br />
independent assay laboratory which shall be determined jointly by AZERGYZIL and Contractor.<br /><br />

or container, as the case may be, as well as all impurities contained therein.<br /><br />

marked with the fineness and stamp of an acceptable assayer, must be accompanied by a certificate<br /><br />
issued by an acceptable assayer stating the serial number of the bar and the fineness. If a bar bears<br /><br />
more than one assay stamp, preference shall be given to the British assay and where a bar bears no<br /><br />
British assay, the lowest figure will be taken. Gold said to be 1000 fine will be marked down to<br /><br />
999.9 fine.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(d)<br /><br />
Çàùèðè ýþðêÿì: Êöë÷ÿëÿð ýþç îõøàìàëû, îíëàðäà ÷àòëàãëàð âÿ éà äèýÿð êÿëÿ-êþòöðëÿð,<br /><br />
ãàòëàð, ùÿääÿí àðòûã áöçöøìÿëÿð îëìàìàëû, ùàáåëÿ éöíýöëëöê òÿñ'èðè áàüûøëàìàëû âÿ ðàùàò<br /><br />
ãàáëàøäûðûëìàëûäûð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(d)<br /><br />
Appearance: Bars should be of good appearance, free from surface cavities or other<br /><br />
irregularities, layering and excessive shrinkage, and must be easy to handle and convenient to<br /><br />
stack.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 13<br /><br />
VALUATION OF COMMERCIAL PRODUCT<br /><br />
13.1 For the purposes of this Agreement, the prices for Commercial Products shall be the<br /><br />
Market Price F.O.B. the Processing Point(s), expressed in Dollars and payable within thirty (30)<br /><br />
days after the date of the bill of lading (in the case of exports) or invoice (in the case of<br /><br />
Commercial Products not exported), as determined below for each Calendar Quarter. A Market<br /><br />
Price shall be determined for each component of Mining Product.<br /><br />
13.2 The Market Price(s) applicable to extraction of Commercial Products produced during a<br /><br />
Calendar Quarter shall be calculated at the end of said Calendar Quarter and shall be equal to the<br /><br />
weighted average of the prices obtained for Commercial Products from the Mining Property during<br /><br />
said Calendar Quarter, by CONTRACTOR and by AZERGYZIL, from independent buyers,<br /><br />
adjusted for differences in F.O.B. delivery terms and payment conditions, provided that the<br /><br />
quantities sold to independent buyers during the Calendar Quarter concerned equal at least one-third<br /><br />
of the total quantities of Mining Product from the Mining Property sold during said Calendar<br /><br />
Quarter.<br /><br />
13.3 In the event sales to independent buyers are not made, or do not represent one-third (1/3) of<br /><br />
the total quantities of Mining Product sold during the applicable Calendar Quarter, the Market<br /><br />
Price(s) shall be determined in the following manner:<br /><br />
(a)<br /><br />
For all metallic Commercial Products, the reference Market Price of each component of<br /><br />
metallic Mining Product shall be the average Quarterly price as posted by Englehard Minerals &<br /><br />
Chemical Corp. (or comparable mineral refining and extraction company); and<br /><br />
<br /><br />

13.4 The following transactions shall be excluded from the calculation of the Market Price(s) of<br /><br />

(b)<br /><br />

or partially made for reasons other than the usual economic incentives involved in Commercial<br /><br />

such as but not limited to gold or silver, for purposes of establishing reserves, speculating on<br /><br />
commodity prices or for any other purpose.<br /><br />

each sale the identity of the buyer, the quantities sold and the delivery and payment terms.<br /><br />

determine in accordance with the provisions of Article 13.2 or Article 13.3 the Market Price(s)<br /><br />

13.6 Current allocations of Cost Recovery Commercial Products and the sharing of Profit<br /><br />
Commercial Products during a Calendar Quarter shall be based on the Quarterly Market Price(s)<br /><br />
last determined. When a new Quarterly Market Price(s) is determined, that Commercial Products<br /><br />
value shall be applied retroactively for the Calendar Quarter whose sales the new Commercial<br /><br />
Products Market Price(s) reflects, and adjustments shall then be made in the accounts by<br /><br />
increasing or decreasing the amount of unrecovered costs, as applicable, to reflect the retroactive<br /><br />
application of the new Commercial Products value.<br /><br />

ARTICLE 14<br /><br />
<br /><br />
ÈÄÕÀË Âß ÈÕÐÀÆ<br /><br />

14.1 For the purposes of Mining Operations in accordance with this Agreement Contractor, its<br /><br />
agents and Sub-contractors, shall have the right to import into the Azerbaijan Republic free of any<br /><br />
Taxes and restrictions necessary equipment, rigs, machinery, tools, vehicles, spare parts, materials<br /><br />
and goods, provided, however, that with respect to the purchase thereof Contractor shall give<br /><br />
preference to Azerbaijani suppliers in those cases in which such Azerbaijani suppliers are in all<br /><br />
material respects competitive in price, quality and availability with those available from other<br /><br />
sources; in this respect Azerbaijani suppliers shall mean companies and entities registered and<br /><br />
incorporated in the Azerbaijan Republic, legally operating in the Azerbaijan Republic.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

the results. AZERGYZIL'S representative with no right to vote shall participate at every bid stage.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
(j)<br /><br />
Each Contractor Party shall have the right to sell or transfer any Fixed Assets at market<br /><br />
prices which it owns without regard to book value of the Fixed Assets.<br /><br />
(k)<br /><br />
Each Contractor Party may carry forward without any limitation or restriction all Balance<br /><br />
Losses arising in any Calendar Year. Such losses may be carried forward to the following<br /><br />
Calendar Year and to subsequent Calendar Years, one at a time in chronological order, and shall<br /><br />
offset such Contractor Party's Balance Profit in full without limitation or restriction in such<br /><br />
Calendar Year(s) until such time as the loss is wholly offset against such Contractor Party's<br /><br />
Balance Profit.<br /><br />
(l)<br /><br />
Should any Contractor Party assign all or any part of its interest in the Agreement, the<br /><br />
assigning Contractor Party shall have the option to elect to have the assignee deduct against its<br /><br />
future Balance Profits all (or a proportional part, if only part is assigned) of the balance of the<br /><br />
unrelieved Balance Losses of the assignor Contractor Party arising from the assigned interest in<br /><br />
the Agreement.<br /><br />
(m)<br /><br />
For the purpose of computing the Contractor Party's Taxable Profit/(Loss), all costs<br /><br />
incurred by the Contractor Party in connection with Mining Operations (including but not limited<br /><br />
to costs incurred directly or indirectly in connection with technical work in the Azerbaijan<br /><br />
Republic or elsewhere and costs incurred by representative offices in the Azerbaijan Republic of<br /><br />
the Contractor Party) which were incurred prior to the Effective Date, shall be deemed to have been<br /><br />
incurred on such date.<br /><br />
16.4 Accounting and Returns<br /><br />
(a)<br /><br />
Each Contractor Party shall:<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
maintain its tax books and records exclusively in Dollars;<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
recognize in its tax accounts income and expenditure at the time that such items<br /><br />
would be recorded in accordance with the accounting principles adopted in the Azerbaijan<br /><br />
Republic; i.e. on a cash receipts and disbursements basis;<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
draw up its financial statements and Profit Tax returns exclusively in Dollars and<br /><br />
submit one set of accounts for the Calendar Year consisting of a tax balance sheet and profit and<br /><br />
loss account, together with one Profit Tax computation for the Calendar Year reflecting its Mining<br /><br />
Activities of all of its Permanent Establishments in the Azerbaijan Republic;<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(m)<br /><br />

(vi)<br /><br />
beginning in the first Calendar Year in which it estimates it will earn a Taxable<br /><br />
Profit, pay estimated Profit Tax for each Calendar Quarter based upon its estimate of its Taxable<br /><br />
Profit for such Calendar Quarter and for the preceding Calendar Quarters in such Calendar Year.<br /><br />
Estimated Profit Tax shall be paid on or before twenty-five (25) days following the end of the<br /><br />
relevant Calendar Quarter and shall be accompanied by a calculation in the form as set out in<br /><br />
Article 16.3 (a). In calculating the estimated Profit Tax for a Calendar Quarter, each Contractor<br /><br />
Party may utilize the Annual Work Program along with any other information which it deems<br /><br />
appropriate.<br /><br />
(b)<br /><br />
Upon filing the final Profit Tax return for a Calendar Year, estimated Profit Tax paid with<br /><br />
respect to the Calendar Quarters during such Calendar Year shall be credited against the final<br /><br />
Profit Tax as calculated on the final Profit Tax return. Any overpayment shall be refunded to the<br /><br />
Contractor Party within ten (10) days following the date the Contractor Party's final Profit Tax<br /><br />
return (for such Calendar Quarters or Quarters estimated Profit Tax payment(s)) is submitted. Any<br /><br />
underpayment shall be paid by the Contractor Party within ten (10) days following the date such<br /><br />
final Profit Tax return is submitted. In any event, the final Profit Tax for a Calendar Year as<br /><br />
calculated in the Profit Tax return shall be payable no later than 25 March of the following<br /><br />
Calendar Year.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(c)<br /><br />
All estimated and final payments (and refunds of overpayments) of Profit Tax and any<br /><br />
interest and penalty sanctions thereon as described in Article 16.4(d) below shall be made in<br /><br />
Dollars.<br /><br />
(d)<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
The filing of the Profit Tax returns and payment of Profit Tax hereunder for a<br /><br />
Calendar Year shall be deemed to be a final and conclusive settlement of all Profit Tax liabilities<br /><br />
for that Calendar Year upon the date thirty-six (36) months from the date the Profit Tax return for<br /><br />
such Calendar Year was filed. The Contractor Party and the Tax Inspectorate may, by mutual<br /><br />
agreement, extend this period.<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
The Tax Inspectorate shall have the authority to conduct an audit of each Contractor<br /><br />
Party's Profit Tax return for each Calendar Year. Upon completing such audit, the Tax Inspectorate<br /><br />
shall discuss any proposed adjustments with the Contractor Party and, where appropriate, issue a<br /><br />
notice of additional Profit Tax due or a notice of refund. Any agreed underpayments or<br /><br />
overpayments of Profit Tax shall be paid within ten (10) days following receipt by the Contractor<br /><br />
Party of the appropriate notice. If the Contractor Party and the Tax Inspectorate are unable to agree<br /><br />
upon the amount of Profit Tax underpaid or overpaid, the issue shall be submitted to arbitration<br /><br />
applying the principles contained in Article 21.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
Upon a final determination that there has been either an underpayment or<br /><br />
overpayment of Profit Tax on the Contractor Party's final Profit Tax return for a Calendar Year,<br /><br />
the Contractor Party shall pay to the Tax Inspectorate (or, in the case of a refund of an<br /><br />
overpayment, receive from the Tax Inspectorate) interest on the amount of the underpayment or<br /><br />
overpayment at the rate of LIBOR plus four (4) percent (such LIBOR rate prevailing on the day<br /><br />
before payment). Such interest shall be computed from 25th March in the Calendar Year the final<br /><br />
Profit Tax return was filed until the date the Profit Tax is paid or refunded to the Contractor Party.<br /><br />

èäàðÿëÿðèíÿ þäÿéèð. Áó âåðýèëÿð ùÿìèí Õàðèæè ñóáïîäðàò÷ûíûí âåðýè ìÿñ’óëèééÿòèíè, ùàáåëÿ îíóí<br /><br />
áÿéàííàìÿ òÿãäèì åòìÿê âÿ áöòöí Âåðýèëÿðè þäÿìÿê þùäÿëèêëÿðèíè òàìàìèëÿ ÿùàòÿ åäèð.<br /><br />
(ii) Ùå÷ áèð Ïîäðàò÷û òÿðÿô þç Ñóáïîäðàò÷ûëàðûíûí ùÿð ùàíñû âåðýèëÿðè òóòìàäûãëàðû âÿ éà<br /><br />

ýþòöðìöð.<br /><br />

áèð Âåðýè ãîéóëìóð âÿ îíëàðäàí Âåðýè òóòóëìóð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
16.5 Employee Taxes<br /><br />
(a) All employees of each Contractor Party and its Affiliates shall be liable to pay the Azerbaijan<br /><br />
Republic personal income Tax regardless of the length of stay and it shall be based only on their<br /><br />
income earned as a direct result of their employment in the Azerbaijan Republic on a nondiscriminatory nature, subject to any applicable Double Tax Treaty.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv) In addition to interest payable as computed under (iii) above, each Contractor Party<br /><br />
shall be subject to only the following penalty sanctions with respect of Taxes:<br /><br />
(aa) if a Contractor Party fails to file a final Profit Tax return, it shall be liable for a<br /><br />
penalty of one hundred and ten (110) percent of the Profit Tax required to be paid with such Profit<br /><br />
Tax return.<br /><br />
(bb) if the amount of Profit Tax due as shown on the final Profit Tax return for a<br /><br />
Calendar Year was understated due to fraud by the Contractor Party, it shall be liable for a penalty<br /><br />
of two hundred (200) percent of the amount of the understatement.<br /><br />
(e) The Tax Inspectorate will issue to the Contractor Party official tax receipts evidencing the<br /><br />
payment of estimated or final Profit Tax within ten (10) days of any such payment. Such tax<br /><br />
receipts shall state the date and amount of such payment, the currency in which such payment was<br /><br />
made and any other particulars customary in the Azerbaijan Republic for such receipts.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(b) Each Contractor Party and its Affiliate shall only make contributions to Azerbaijan State social<br /><br />
insurance and similar payments (including but not limited to contributions to the pension funds,<br /><br />
the unemployment fund, the social insurance fund and the medical fund) with respect to permanent<br /><br />
employees who are citizens of the Azerbaijan Republic.<br /><br />
16.6 Taxation of Sub-contractors<br /><br />
(a) Foreign Sub-contractors shall be taxed as follows:<br /><br />
(i) Foreign Sub-contractors carrying on business in the Azerbaijan Republic in connection<br /><br />
with Mining Activities shall be deemed to earn a taxable profit of twenty- five (25) percent of the<br /><br />
payments received for work and services in connection with Mining Activities in the Azerbaijan<br /><br />
Republic and such profit shall be subject to tax at the rate of thirty-two (32) percent, resulting in a<br /><br />
total tax obligation of eight (8) percent of such payments. Any person making such payments shall<br /><br />
therefore withhold tax from such payments and shall pay such withheld taxes within thirty (30)<br /><br />
days from the date of payment. Such taxes withheld shall fully satisfy such Foreign Subcontractors tax compliance, filing obligations and liability for all Taxes.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii) a Contractor Party shall have no liability or responsibility for any Taxes which its Subcontractors do not withhold or pay or for any other failure of such Sub-contractors to comply with<br /><br />
the laws of the Azerbaijan Republic.<br /><br />
(iii) no Taxes shall be imposed or withheld with respect to payments to any Foreign Subcontractor other than as provided in this Article 16.6(a).<br /><br />
<br /><br />

ëÿíýèòìÿñè Ôîðñ-ìàúîð ùàëëàðûíäàí èðÿëè ýÿëäèêäÿ âÿ éà ùÿìèí ùàëëàð íÿòèæÿñèíäÿ áàø âåðäèêäÿ,<br /><br />
ìÿñ’óëèééÿòÿ ñÿáÿá îëìóð. Ôîðñ-ìàúîð ùàëëàðû î äåìÿêäèð êè, ùÿð ùàíñû áèð ùàäèñÿ Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç<br /><br />

òÿäáèðëÿð ýþðöëñÿ äÿ áó ùàäèñÿ âÿ éà îíóí íÿòèæÿëÿðè, î æöìëÿäÿí, ëàêèí áóíëàðëà<br /><br />
ìÿùäóäëàøäûðûëìàäàí, ôþâãÿëàäÿ ùàäèñÿëÿð, òÿáèè ôÿëàêÿòëÿð (ìÿñÿëÿí, èëäûðûì âóðìàñû âÿ<br /><br />
çÿëçÿëÿ), ìöùàðèáÿëÿð (å’ëàí åäèëìèø, éàõóä å’ëàí åäèëìÿìèø) âÿ éà äèýÿð ùÿðáè ÿìÿëèééàòëàð,<br /><br />
éàíüûíëàð, öñéàíëàð, òåððîð÷óëóã àêòëàðû, âÿòÿíäàø èüòèøàøëàðû, ìàëýþíäÿðÿíèí éåýàíÿ îëìàñû<br /><br />

ãàðøûñûíû àëìàã ö÷öí ùÿð æöð ëàçûìè ùöãóãè ñÿ’éëÿð ýþñòÿðÿæÿêäèð. Ùÿð ùàíñû Ôîðñ-ìàúîð<br /><br />
âÿçèééÿòè ìþâæóä îëäóãäà âÿ éà éàðàíäûãäà îíóí òÿ’ñèðèíÿ ìÿ’ðóç ãàëàí Òÿðÿô Ôîðñ-ìàúîð<br /><br />
âÿçèééÿòèíèí õàðàêòåðèíè òÿñâèð åòìÿêëÿ (âÿ ìöâàôèã ñöáóò òÿãäèì åòìÿêëÿ) äÿðùàë äèýÿð Òÿðÿôÿ<br /><br />
éàçûëû áèëäèðèø âåðÿæÿê âÿ ùÿìèí Ôîðñ-ìàúîð âÿçèééÿòèíèí òÿ’ñèðèíè àðàäàí ãàëäûðìàã, éàõóä<br /><br />
éöíýöëëÿøäèðìÿê ö÷öí ëàçûìè ùöãóãè ñÿ’éëÿð ýþñòÿðÿðÿê, íÿ ìöìêöíäöðñÿ åäÿæÿêäèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
19.1 Non-performance or delays in performance on the part of any Party of its obligations (or<br /><br />
any part thereof) under this Agreement, other than the obligation to pay money, shall be excused if<br /><br />
occasioned or caused by Force Majeure. Force Majeure means any event which prevents, hinders<br /><br />
or impedes Mining Operations and is beyond the ability of the affected Party to control such event<br /><br />
or its consequences using reasonable efforts, including without limitation, extraordinary events,<br /><br />
natural disasters (for example lighting and earthquake), wars (declared or undeclared) or other<br /><br />
military activity, fire, insurrections, rebellions, acts of terrorism, riot, civil commotion, sole<br /><br />
supplier or laws, treaties, rules, regulations, decrees, orders, actions or inactions of any<br /><br />
governmental authority (inside or outside of the Azerbaijan Republic) which prevent hinder or<br /><br />
impede Contractors conduct of operations or which substantially impairs or threatens Contractors<br /><br />
rights under this Agreement (as determined by the arbitration); Every Party will make all<br /><br />
reasonable and lawful endeavors to avert the emergence of Force Majeure events. Upon the<br /><br />
existence or occurrence of any Force Majeure event, the Party affected shall give prompt notice to<br /><br />
the other Parties specifying the event of Force Majeure (and providing evidence thereof) and shall<br /><br />
do all things possible using reasonable lawful efforts to remove or mitigate the effect of the Force<br /><br />
Majeure event.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />
Economic Stabilization<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The rights and interests accruing to Contractor (or its assignees) under this Agreement and<br /><br />
its Sub-contractors under this Agreement shall not be amended, modified or reduced without the<br /><br />
prior consent of Contractor. In the event that any Governmental Authority invokes any present or<br /><br />
future law, treaty, intergovernmental agreement, decree or administrative order which contravenes<br /><br />
the provisions of this Agreement or adversely or positively affects the rights or interests of<br /><br />
Contractor hereunder, including, but not limited to, any changes in tax legislation, regulations, or<br /><br />
administrative practice, or jurisdictional changes pertaining to the Contract Area, the terms of this<br /><br />
Agreement shall be adjusted to re-establish the economic equilibrium of the Parties, and if the<br /><br />
rights or interests of Contractor have been adversely affected, then AZERGYZIL shall indemnify<br /><br />
Contractor (and its assignees) for any disbenefit, deterioration in economic circumstances, loss or<br /><br />
damages that ensue therefrom.<br /><br />

(iii)<br /><br />
After providing thirty (30) days prior written notice to the other Party of intent to<br /><br />
arbitrate, either AZERGYZIL or Contractor may initiate arbitration (the Party initiating the<br /><br />
arbitration shall hereinafter be called the First Party) submitting a request for arbitration to the<br /><br />
Secretary General of the Permanent Court of Arbitration in the Hague, as provided in the Rules,<br /><br />
and appointing an arbitrator who shall be identified in said request. Within thirty (30) days of<br /><br />
receipt of a copy of the request the other Party to the dispute (Second Party) shall respond,<br /><br />
identifying the arbitrator that it has selected. If the Second Party does not so appoint its arbitrator,<br /><br />
the Secretary General of the Permanent Court of Arbitration in the Hague shall appoint a second<br /><br />
arbitrator in accordance with the Rules.<br /><br />

Conduct of Operations<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Ïîäðàò÷û Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ÿìÿëèééàòëàðûíû æàí-áàøëà, ëàçûìè ñÿìÿðÿëèëèê âÿ òÿùëöêÿñèçëèêëÿ,<br /><br />
Àçÿðáàéæàí Ðåñïóáëèêàñûíûí òÿùëöêÿñèçëèê òåõíèêàñûíà âÿ ÿòðàô ìöùèòèí ìöùàôèçÿñèíÿ äàèð<br /><br />
ìþâæóä ãàíóíâåðèæèëèéèíÿ, ùàáåëÿ Áåéíÿëõàëã ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ñÿíàéåñè ñòàíäàðòëàðûíà óéüóí<br /><br />

äàèð ãàíóíâåðèæèëèéèíÿ çèää îëìàéàí äÿðÿæÿäÿ àïàðûð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor shall conduct the Mining Operations in a diligent, safe and efficient manner in<br /><br />
accordance with existing safety and environmental legislation of the Azerbaijan Republic and<br /><br />
International Mining Industry Standards and experience to the extent they shall not be in conflict<br /><br />
with safety and environmental legislation of the Azerbaijan Republic.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Ïîäðàò÷û ìÿùäóäèééÿò ãîéìàäàí éåðèí öñòö, éåðèí òÿêè, ùàâà, ýþëëÿð, ÷àéëàð, ôëîðà âÿ<br /><br />
ôàóíà, êÿíä òÿñÿððöôàòû áèòêèëÿðè, äèýÿð òÿáèè åùòèéàòëàð âÿ ÿìëàê äàõèë îëìàãëà áöòþâëöêëÿ<br /><br />
ÿòðàô ìöùèòèí ìöâàçèíÿòèíèí ùÿð ùàíñû ïîòåíñèàë ïîçóíòóëàðûíû ìèíèìóìà åíäèðìÿê ö÷öí<br /><br />
áöòöí çÿðóðè òÿäáèðëÿðè ýþðöð. Òÿäáèðëÿðèí íþâáÿëèëèéè áó ñûðà èëÿ ìöÿééÿí åäèëèð: ùÿéàòûí<br /><br />
ìöùàôèçÿñè, ÿòðàô ìöùèòèí ìöùàôèçÿñè âÿ ÿìëàêûí ìöùàôèçÿñè.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Contractor shall take all reasonable actions to minimize any potential disturbance to the<br /><br />
general environment, including without limitation the surface, subsurface, air, lakes, rivers, animal<br /><br />
life, plant life, crops and other natural resources and property. The order of priority for actions<br /><br />
shall be the protection of life, environment and property.<br /><br />

îðãàíëàðû ãàðøûñûíäà ùåñàáàò âåðèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
In the event of emergency and accidents which damage or might damage the environment,<br /><br />
Contractor shall promptly notify the State Committee of the Azerbaijan Republic on Ecology and<br /><br />
Control over the Use of Natural Resources and AZERGYZIL of such circumstances and of its first<br /><br />
steps to remedy this situation and the results of said efforts. Contractor shall use all reasonable<br /><br />
endeavors to take immediate steps to bring the emergency situation under control and protect<br /><br />
against loss of life and loss of or damage to property and prevent harm to natural resources and to<br /><br />
the general environment. Contractor shall also report to AZERGYZIL and appropriate<br /><br />
Governmental Authorities on the measures taken.<br /><br />

General Provisions<br /><br />

òÿøêèë åäèðëÿð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
The purpose of this Accounting Procedure is to establish a fair and equitable method for<br /><br />
determining charges and credits applicable to Mining Operations under the Agreement and to<br /><br />
provide a method for controlling expenditure against approved budgets. For purposes of this<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure any reference to Contractor shall be deemed to include the Operating<br /><br />
Company and respective Affiliates, as the context may imply. The Parties agree that if any of such<br /><br />
methods prove to be unfair or inequitable to any of the Parties then the Parties will meet and in<br /><br />
good faith endeavor to agree on such changes as are necessary to correct any unfairness or<br /><br />
inequity.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

<br /><br />
1.1<br /><br />

Definitions<br /><br />

òÿðìèíëÿðÿ áåëÿ ìÿ’íàëàð âåðèëèð:<br /><br />

For the purposes of this Accounting Procedure the following terms shall have the following<br /><br />
meanings:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
Ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí àïàðûëìàñû ãàéäàñû - ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí áó ßëàâÿäÿ<br /><br />
ýþñòÿðèëÿí ïðèíñèïëÿðè, ìåòîäëàðû âÿ öñóëëàðû äåìÿêäèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(i)<br /><br />
Accounting Procedure shall mean the accounting principles, practices and<br /><br />
procedures set forth in this Appendix.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />
Ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí ãÿáóë îëóíìóø ìåòîäëàðû - ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí áåéíÿëõàëã<br /><br />
ïðàêòèêàäà ùàìûëûãëà ãÿáóë âÿ òÿñäèã åäèëìèø ïðèíñèïëÿðè, ìåòîäëàðû âÿ öñóëëàðû äåìÿêäèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(ii)<br /><br />

procedures that are generally accepted and recognized in the international practice.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
Àðòàí ìÿáëÿüëÿð - ó÷îò äþâðö ãóðòàðìàçäàí ÿââÿë îëìóø ùàäèñÿëÿð âÿ<br /><br />
ÿìÿëèééàòëàð íÿòèæÿñèíäÿ ó÷îò äþâðö ãóðòàðäûãäàí ñîíðà þäÿíèëÿæÿéè âÿ éà àëûíàæàüû<br /><br />
ýþçëÿíèëÿí ìÿáëÿüëÿð äåìÿêäèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iii)<br /><br />
Accruals means amounts which are expected to be paid or received after the end of<br /><br />
an accounting period as a result of events and transactions prior to the end of the said accounting<br /><br />
period.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
Àðòìà ïðèíñèïè - ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí åëÿ ïðèíñèïè äåìÿêäèð êè, ùÿìèí ïðèíñèïÿ<br /><br />
ýþðÿ ÿìÿëèééàòëàðûí íÿòèæÿëÿðè, ìàëèééÿ øÿðàèòèíÿ âÿ ýÿëèðÿ òÿ’ñèðè ñàäÿæÿ îëàðàã ÿìÿëèééàòëàð<br /><br />
öçðÿ íàüä ùàãã-ùåñàá ÷ÿêèëÿíäÿ äåéèë, ùÿìèí ÿìÿëèééàòëàð àïàðûëàíäà ìöùàñèáàò<br /><br />
êèòàáëàðûíäà ãåéä îëóíóð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(iv)<br /><br />
Accruals Basis means the basis of accounting which records the effect of<br /><br />
transactions on financial conditions and income when the transactions take place, not merely when<br /><br />
they are settled in cash.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />
Êàññà ïðèíñèïè - Ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí åëÿ ïðèíñèïè äåìÿêäèð êè, ùÿìèí ïðèíñèïÿ<br /><br />

ùàãã-ùåñàá ÷ÿêèëÿíäÿ ìöùàñèáàò êèòàáëàðûíäà ãåéä îëóíóð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(v)<br /><br />

on financial conditions and income when they are settled in cash.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
(vi)<br /><br />
Ãàïàëû ó÷îò ïðèíñèïè - ìöùàñèáàò ó÷îòóíóí åëÿ ïðèíñèïè äåìÿêäèð êè, ùÿìèí<br /><br />

<br /><br />
(vi)<br /><br />

<br /><br />
(vii) Ìàòåðèàëëàð âÿ àâàäàíëûã - Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ÿìÿëèééàòëàðûíäà èøëÿäèëìÿê ö÷öí ÿëäÿ<br /><br />

Accounts<br /><br />
<br /><br />

accordance with this Accounting Procedure (Mining Operations Account).<br /><br />

Mining Operations Account.<br /><br />

<br /><br />
The accounts of the Mining Operations, together with the auditors report thereon, shall be<br /><br />
submitted to AZERGYZIL by Contractor no later than seven (7) months following the end of each<br /><br />
Calendar Year. AZERGYZIL may, by giving notice to that effect to Contractor not later than<br /><br />
twelve (12) months following the end of the subject Calendar Year, request an audit of the<br /><br />
accounts for such Calendar Year. Such audits shall be carried out by a firm of internationally<br /><br />
recognized independent accountants selected by AZERGYZIL. The cost of such audit shall be<br /><br />
included to the Operational Costs and shall be conducted in such a manner as not to interfere<br /><br />
unduly with ongoing operations. Unless AZERGYZIL notifies Contractor in writing before<br /><br />
twenty-four (24) months following the subject Calendar Year either that it has an objection to the<br /><br />
said accounts or that there is evidence of Contractors Willful Misconduct (details of which shall be<br /><br />
included in said notice), the accounts for such Calendar Year shall be deemed to have been<br /><br />
approved as on that date. Any objection to the accounts raised by AZERGYZIL shall, unless<br /><br />
settled by agreement among the Parties, be submitted to arbitration in accordance with the<br /><br />
Arbitration Procedure. In the event the arbitration award sustains any of AZERGYZIL'S<br /><br />
objections to the account, the Mining Operating Account shall be adjusted accordingly.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

structure or legal existence of AZERGYZIL shall not affect the obligations of the Government<br /><br />
hereunder. The Government shall, throughout the entire duration of the Agreement, ensure that the<br /><br />

DESIGN STANDARDS AND SPECIFICATIONS<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Ìþâæóä ãóðüóëàðûí ìîäèôèêàñèéàñû ïðîãðàìëàðû ÷ÿð÷èâÿñèíäÿ ãóðàøäûðûëàí éåíè ì’äÿí-ôèëèç<br /><br />
îáéåêòëÿðèíèí âÿ àâäàíëûüûíûí ùàìûñû Áåéíÿëõàëã Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ñÿíàéåñèíèí ìöàñèð ñòàíäàðòëàðû<br /><br />
öçðÿ ëàéèùÿëÿøäèðèëÿæÿêäèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
All new mining facilities and all new equipment added as part of a modification program to<br /><br />
existing facilities, will be designed in accordance with current International Mining Industry<br /><br />
Standards.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Ùÿð Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç éàòàüûíäàêû ìþâæóä ãóðüóëàð òèêèíòè çàìàíû òÿòáèã îëóíàí ñòàíäàðòëàð öçðÿ<br /><br />
ëàéèùÿëÿøäèðèëìèøäèð. Éåíè àâàäàíëûüûí òÿùëöêÿñèçëèéè ö÷öí Ïîäðàò÷ûíûí çÿðóðè ñàéäûüû<br /><br />
ùàëëàðäàí áàøãà, îíëàð Áåéíÿëõàëã Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ñÿíàéåñè ñòàíäàðòëàðûíà óéüóí îëàðàã<br /><br />
ìîäåðíëÿøäèðèëìÿéÿæÿêäèð.<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Existing facilities on each Mining Property were designed to the standards appropriate at the time<br /><br />
of their construction. They will not be modified to comply with International Mining Industry<br /><br />
Standards except where determined necessary by Contractor for the safe operation of new<br /><br />
equipment.<br /><br />
<br /><br />

INTERNATIONAL MINING INDUSTRY STANDARDS<br /><br />
<br /><br />
Áåéíÿëõàëã Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ñÿíàéåñè ñòàíäàðòëàðû åëÿ ïðàêòèêà, öñóëëàð, òåõíîëîýèéà âÿ<br /><br />
ôÿàëèééÿòäèð êè, Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ñÿíàéåñèíèí áöòöí ñàùÿëÿðèíäÿ âèæäàíëà ÷àëûøàí ìÿ’äÿí<br /><br />
îïåðàòîðëàðû òÿðÿôèíäÿí ùÿéàòà êå÷èðèëèð âÿ àøàüûäàêû òÿøêèëàòëàðûí öçâö îëàí, éàõóä îíëàðäàí<br /><br />
ùÿð ùàíñû áèðèíèí ïðèíñèïëÿðèíÿ ÿìÿë åäÿí, Ìÿ’äÿí-ôèëèç ñÿíàéåñèíèí òåõíèêè æÿùÿòäÿí ñÿðèøòÿëè<br /><br />
ìöòÿõÿññèñëÿðè òÿðÿôèíäÿí òÿòáèã îëóíàí âÿ ùàìûëûãëà ãÿáóë åäèëÿí éöêñÿê ñÿíàéå ñòàíäàðòëàðû<br /><br />
ñàéûëûð:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
International Mining Industry Standards are those practices, procedures, techniques and<br /><br />
activities carried out by prudent mining operators in all aspects of their mineral industry<br /><br />
activities and which are generally accepted as being of the highest industry standards by<br /><br />
technically competent mining professionals who are members of or adhere to the principles<br /><br />
of any of the following associations:<br /><br />
<br /><br />
IMM - Ìÿ’äÿí âÿ Ìåòàëëóðýèéà Ñÿíàéåñè Ìöùÿíäèñëÿðè Èíñòèòóòó (Ëîíäîí)<br /><br />
